NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
Geo fabrics India private Limited, Chennai.
It is hereby notified to the general Public that the company has passed resolution to wind up the Company by members
voluntary winding up under section 484 of the Companies Act, 1956 and Mr. S. Sandeep, Practicing Company Secretary
having office at No. 53, Ist Main Road, G1, Sneha Apartments, R. A. Puram, Chennai-600 028 is appointed as liquidator
of the Company for the purpose of winding up of the Company.
Chennai-600 028,
18th November 2011.

Ms. THANKAM JOHN,
S. SANDEEP & ASSOCIATES,
Company Secretaries.
